   <script src="https://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?v=3.exp&amp;libraries=places&amp;key=AIzaSyDGHxMGbuTsXJF5cWmQ-DrgG1UfGvQ83BM">

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $('#search').ready(function() {
         var vinput = $('#veranstalter');
         vinput.on('input',function(){
             if ($.trim($(vinput).val()) == ''){
                 $('#q_event_user_id_eq').val('');
             }
         });
 
         // Geolocation
         var patt1=new RegExp(/^[\d]+$/); //nur Zahlen
         var GeoCoded = {done: false};
         var input = document.getElementById('stadt');
         var autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(input);
         // autocomplete.setTypes(['(cities)']); nur nach städten suchen
         autocomplete.setComponentRestrictions({'country': 'de'});
 
         $('#term_search').on('submit',function(e){
 
             if(GeoCoded.done){
                 return true;
             }
             e.preventDefault();
             var address = document.getElementById('stadt').value;
             if( (patt1.test(address)) || address.length == 0 || address == "aktuelle Position") {
                 GeoCoded.done = true;
                 $('#stadt').val('');
                 $('#lat').val('');
                 $('#lng').val('');
                 $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                 $('#suche_kreis').val('');
                 $('#term_search').submit();
             }
             // console.log('submit stopped');
             else{
 
                 var geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
                 $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',true);
 
 
                 geocoder.geocode({
                     'address': address,
                     'componentRestrictions': {'country': 'de'}
                 },function (results, status) {
                     if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
                       $('#lat').val('');
                       $('#lng').val('');
                       $('#stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_kreis').val('');
 
                       for (var i = 0; i < results.length; i++) {
                         var place = results[i];
                         //if (results[i].types[0] === "locality" || results[i].types[0] === "administrative_area_level_1") { //nur nach städten suchen
                         $('#lat').val(place.geometry.location.lat());
                         $('#lng').val(place.geometry.location.lng());
                         //if you only want to submit in the event of successful geocoding, you can only trigger submission here.
                         GeoCoded.done = true;
                         $('#stadt').val(place.formatted_address);
 
                         for (var j=0;j< place.address_components.length;j++) {
                           var place_component = place.address_components[j];
                           for (var k = 0; k < place_component.types.length; k++) {
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "sublocality") {
                               ort = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(ort);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "locality") {
                               stadt = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(stadt);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "administrative_area_level_3") {
                               landkreis = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_kreis').val(landkreis);
                             }
                           }
                         }
 
                         $('#term_search').submit();
                         return;
                       }
                     }
                         // console.log("Geocode was not successful for the following reason: " + status);
                         // $('#searchbutton').val("Ort nicht gefunden");
                         alert("Der Ort wurde nicht gefunden");
                         //enable the submit button
                         $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',false);
 
                 });
             }
         });
 
 
         $('#stadt').keyup(function(){
         if( patt1.test($(this).val())){
         $('#radius').css('display', "none");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "none");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "block");
         }
         else{
         $('#radius').css('display', "block");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "block");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "none");
         }
         });
             });
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $('#search').ready(function() {
         var vinput = $('#veranstalter');
         vinput.on('input',function(){
             if ($.trim($(vinput).val()) == ''){
                 $('#q_event_user_id_eq').val('');
             }
         });
 
         // Geolocation
         var patt1=new RegExp(/^[\d]+$/); //nur Zahlen
         var GeoCoded = {done: false};
         var input = document.getElementById('stadt');
         var autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(input);
         // autocomplete.setTypes(['(cities)']); nur nach städten suchen
         autocomplete.setComponentRestrictions({'country': 'de'});
 
         $('#term_search').on('submit',function(e){
 
             if(GeoCoded.done){
                 return true;
             }
             e.preventDefault();
             var address = document.getElementById('stadt').value;
             if( (patt1.test(address)) || address.length == 0 || address == "aktuelle Position") {
                 GeoCoded.done = true;
                 $('#stadt').val('');
                 $('#lat').val('');
                 $('#lng').val('');
                 $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                 $('#suche_kreis').val('');
                 $('#term_search').submit();
             }
             // console.log('submit stopped');
             else{
 
                 var geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
                 $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',true);
 
 
                 geocoder.geocode({
                     'address': address,
                     'componentRestrictions': {'country': 'de'}
                 },function (results, status) {
                     if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
                       $('#lat').val('');
                       $('#lng').val('');
                       $('#stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_kreis').val('');
 
                       for (var i = 0; i < results.length; i++) {
                         var place = results[i];
                         //if (results[i].types[0] === "locality" || results[i].types[0] === "administrative_area_level_1") { //nur nach städten suchen
                         $('#lat').val(place.geometry.location.lat());
                         $('#lng').val(place.geometry.location.lng());
                         //if you only want to submit in the event of successful geocoding, you can only trigger submission here.
                         GeoCoded.done = true;
                         $('#stadt').val(place.formatted_address);
 
                         for (var j=0;j< place.address_components.length;j++) {
                           var place_component = place.address_components[j];
                           for (var k = 0; k < place_component.types.length; k++) {
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "sublocality") {
                               ort = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(ort);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "locality") {
                               stadt = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(stadt);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "administrative_area_level_3") {
                               landkreis = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_kreis').val(landkreis);
                             }
                           }
                         }
 
                         $('#term_search').submit();
                         return;
                       }
                     }
                         // console.log("Geocode was not successful for the following reason: " + status);
                         // $('#searchbutton').val("Ort nicht gefunden");
                         alert("Der Ort wurde nicht gefunden");
                         //enable the submit button
                         $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',false);
 
                 });
             }
         });
 
 
         $('#stadt').keyup(function(){
         if( patt1.test($(this).val())){
         $('#radius').css('display', "none");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "none");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "block");
         }
         else{
         $('#radius').css('display', "block");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "block");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "none");
         }
         });
             });
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $('#search').ready(function() {
         var vinput = $('#veranstalter');
         vinput.on('input',function(){
             if ($.trim($(vinput).val()) == ''){
                 $('#q_event_user_id_eq').val('');
             }
         });
 
         // Geolocation
         var patt1=new RegExp(/^[\d]+$/); //nur Zahlen
         var GeoCoded = {done: false};
         var input = document.getElementById('stadt');
         var autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(input);
         // autocomplete.setTypes(['(cities)']); nur nach städten suchen
         autocomplete.setComponentRestrictions({'country': 'de'});
 
         $('#term_search').on('submit',function(e){
 
             if(GeoCoded.done){
                 return true;
             }
             e.preventDefault();
             var address = document.getElementById('stadt').value;
             if( (patt1.test(address)) || address.length == 0 || address == "aktuelle Position") {
                 GeoCoded.done = true;
                 $('#stadt').val('');
                 $('#lat').val('');
                 $('#lng').val('');
                 $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                 $('#suche_kreis').val('');
                 $('#term_search').submit();
             }
             // console.log('submit stopped');
             else{
 
                 var geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
                 $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',true);
 
 
                 geocoder.geocode({
                     'address': address,
                     'componentRestrictions': {'country': 'de'}
                 },function (results, status) {
                     if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
                       $('#lat').val('');
                       $('#lng').val('');
                       $('#stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_kreis').val('');
 
                       for (var i = 0; i < results.length; i++) {
                         var place = results[i];
                         //if (results[i].types[0] === "locality" || results[i].types[0] === "administrative_area_level_1") { //nur nach städten suchen
                         $('#lat').val(place.geometry.location.lat());
                         $('#lng').val(place.geometry.location.lng());
                         //if you only want to submit in the event of successful geocoding, you can only trigger submission here.
                         GeoCoded.done = true;
                         $('#stadt').val(place.formatted_address);
 
                         for (var j=0;j< place.address_components.length;j++) {
                           var place_component = place.address_components[j];
                           for (var k = 0; k < place_component.types.length; k++) {
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "sublocality") {
                               ort = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(ort);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "locality") {
                               stadt = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(stadt);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "administrative_area_level_3") {
                               landkreis = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_kreis').val(landkreis);
                             }
                           }
                         }
 
                         $('#term_search').submit();
                         return;
                       }
                     }
                         // console.log("Geocode was not successful for the following reason: " + status);
                         // $('#searchbutton').val("Ort nicht gefunden");
                         alert("Der Ort wurde nicht gefunden");
                         //enable the submit button
                         $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',false);
 
                 });
             }
         });
 
 
         $('#stadt').keyup(function(){
         if( patt1.test($(this).val())){
         $('#radius').css('display', "none");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "none");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "block");
         }
         else{
         $('#radius').css('display', "block");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "block");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "none");
         }
         });
             });
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $('#search').ready(function() {
         var vinput = $('#veranstalter');
         vinput.on('input',function(){
             if ($.trim($(vinput).val()) == ''){
                 $('#q_event_user_id_eq').val('');
             }
         });
 
         // Geolocation
         var patt1=new RegExp(/^[\d]+$/); //nur Zahlen
         var GeoCoded = {done: false};
         var input = document.getElementById('stadt');
         var autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(input);
         // autocomplete.setTypes(['(cities)']); nur nach städten suchen
         autocomplete.setComponentRestrictions({'country': 'de'});
 
         $('#term_search').on('submit',function(e){
 
             if(GeoCoded.done){
                 return true;
             }
             e.preventDefault();
             var address = document.getElementById('stadt').value;
             if( (patt1.test(address)) || address.length == 0 || address == "aktuelle Position") {
                 GeoCoded.done = true;
                 $('#stadt').val('');
                 $('#lat').val('');
                 $('#lng').val('');
                 $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                 $('#suche_kreis').val('');
                 $('#term_search').submit();
             }
             // console.log('submit stopped');
             else{
 
                 var geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
                 $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',true);
 
 
                 geocoder.geocode({
                     'address': address,
                     'componentRestrictions': {'country': 'de'}
                 },function (results, status) {
                     if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
                       $('#lat').val('');
                       $('#lng').val('');
                       $('#stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_kreis').val('');
 
                       for (var i = 0; i < results.length; i++) {
                         var place = results[i];
                         //if (results[i].types[0] === "locality" || results[i].types[0] === "administrative_area_level_1") { //nur nach städten suchen
                         $('#lat').val(place.geometry.location.lat());
                         $('#lng').val(place.geometry.location.lng());
                         //if you only want to submit in the event of successful geocoding, you can only trigger submission here.
                         GeoCoded.done = true;
                         $('#stadt').val(place.formatted_address);
 
                         for (var j=0;j< place.address_components.length;j++) {
                           var place_component = place.address_components[j];
                           for (var k = 0; k < place_component.types.length; k++) {
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "sublocality") {
                               ort = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(ort);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "locality") {
                               stadt = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(stadt);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "administrative_area_level_3") {
                               landkreis = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_kreis').val(landkreis);
                             }
                           }
                         }
 
                         $('#term_search').submit();
                         return;
                       }
                     }
                         // console.log("Geocode was not successful for the following reason: " + status);
                         // $('#searchbutton').val("Ort nicht gefunden");
                         alert("Der Ort wurde nicht gefunden");
                         //enable the submit button
                         $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',false);
 
                 });
             }
         });
 
 
         $('#stadt').keyup(function(){
         if( patt1.test($(this).val())){
         $('#radius').css('display', "none");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "none");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "block");
         }
         else{
         $('#radius').css('display', "block");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "block");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "none");
         }
         });
             });
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $('#search').ready(function() {
         var vinput = $('#veranstalter');
         vinput.on('input',function(){
             if ($.trim($(vinput).val()) == ''){
                 $('#q_event_user_id_eq').val('');
             }
         });
 
         // Geolocation
         var patt1=new RegExp(/^[\d]+$/); //nur Zahlen
         var GeoCoded = {done: false};
         var input = document.getElementById('stadt');
         var autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(input);
         // autocomplete.setTypes(['(cities)']); nur nach städten suchen
         autocomplete.setComponentRestrictions({'country': 'de'});
 
         $('#term_search').on('submit',function(e){
 
             if(GeoCoded.done){
                 return true;
             }
             e.preventDefault();
             var address = document.getElementById('stadt').value;
             if( (patt1.test(address)) || address.length == 0 || address == "aktuelle Position") {
                 GeoCoded.done = true;
                 $('#stadt').val('');
                 $('#lat').val('');
                 $('#lng').val('');
                 $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                 $('#suche_kreis').val('');
                 $('#term_search').submit();
             }
             // console.log('submit stopped');
             else{
 
                 var geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
                 $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',true);
 
 
                 geocoder.geocode({
                     'address': address,
                     'componentRestrictions': {'country': 'de'}
                 },function (results, status) {
                     if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
                       $('#lat').val('');
                       $('#lng').val('');
                       $('#stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_stadt').val('');
                       $('#suche_kreis').val('');
 
                       for (var i = 0; i < results.length; i++) {
                         var place = results[i];
                         //if (results[i].types[0] === "locality" || results[i].types[0] === "administrative_area_level_1") { //nur nach städten suchen
                         $('#lat').val(place.geometry.location.lat());
                         $('#lng').val(place.geometry.location.lng());
                         //if you only want to submit in the event of successful geocoding, you can only trigger submission here.
                         GeoCoded.done = true;
                         $('#stadt').val(place.formatted_address);
 
                         for (var j=0;j< place.address_components.length;j++) {
                           var place_component = place.address_components[j];
                           for (var k = 0; k < place_component.types.length; k++) {
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "sublocality") {
                               ort = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(ort);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "locality") {
                               stadt = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_stadt').val(stadt);
                             }
                             if (place_component.types[k] == "administrative_area_level_3") {
                               landkreis = place_component.long_name;
                               $('#suche_kreis').val(landkreis);
                             }
                           }
                         }
 
                         $('#term_search').submit();
                         return;
                       }
                     }
                         // console.log("Geocode was not successful for the following reason: " + status);
                         // $('#searchbutton').val("Ort nicht gefunden");
                         alert("Der Ort wurde nicht gefunden");
                         //enable the submit button
                         $('#term_search input[type="submit"]').attr('disabled',false);
 
                 });
             }
         });
 
 
         $('#stadt').keyup(function(){
         if( patt1.test($(this).val())){
         $('#radius').css('display', "none");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "none");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "block");
         }
         else{
         $('#radius').css('display', "block");
         // $('#radius_Umkreis').css('display', "block");
         $('#radius_hinweis').css('display', "none");
         }
         });
             });
   </script>
